I placed an order for a tartar control product for my collies in August 2015.  The site claimed the items were in stock while other pet product websites were out of stock.  I'm in luck!  I placed the order and my PayPal account was charged.   Two days later I receive an email stating that the items are on back order with no estimated date of delivery and no offer to cancel the order and refund the money.

I sent a refund request by email and contacted the company by phone requesting the same. Days pass and no refund. I contacted PayPal for a resolution.  The refund eventually was processed.  The time and effort to get this resolved really added up.  This is what happens when companies deliberately sell out of stock product. Starting in early September, I began receiving promotional email from the company, they clearly lost me as a customer, and every time I received one, I would use the "unsubscribe" link to stop it.  It's now mid November and I have made a total of 21 requests via online/email and 4 phone calls to the company that have resulted in ZERO response.  I received another email promotion today November 18 for Black Friday.

This is what you can expect from Healthy Pets:

1. Sells and charges for product they know is not in stock.
2. Lead you to believe a product will be in-stock by stating it was "delayed due to an unexpected and temporary backorder".
3. Completely ignore numerous requests to stop emailing you with promotions.
4. Waste your time.

In my opinion and from my experience, I think the company uses dishonest selling practices, this was no mistake, and they obviously could care less about their customer's time. I would avoid doing business with them.< /Review>

<Review>Just, wow. In LA for a week w my GF son so I scouted the places to eat that our hometown Houston lacks.

This was our last stop prior to going home and I‚Äôm so glad we made it because it was the culinary highlight of our trip.

As a sourdough enthusiast, loved that our breakfast came with the yummy buckwheat sourdough. My only add would be to serve with butter and maybe some interesting jam because buckwheat breads can be less moist and the butter they did put on was a bit too little. The bread was great though!

My son did eggs and bacon and he thought the soft scramble was a perfect execution. I did the eggs baked with the red sauce and added sausage and the sheep‚Äôs cheese (worth the add!) and the dish was an easy ten.

The guy who took our order was a doll and helped me decide what to get from the fifty things I wanted to try. The manager came around to say hi. Helpful smiles everywhere.

I‚Äôm in this happy space and then I see the record that started it all on the wall - Buckingham Nicks. I feel this connection to this wonderful space and the people I‚Äôve never met who made this great food and chose to display this one (1) record on the wall. This would have been my one record also.

< Review>
As expected, the food is like any Del Taco locations.  Thus, no point writing a review on food.  So all the prior reviews on prices, food are probably pointless.  This is a franchise and the price on these items are set similarly across the board

However, there are a few points worth mentioning.  This location needs some cleaning.  The place smells.  I would said, the cleanliness itself lowers the rating by 1 star.  The restroom is so dirty that it is unbearable. For someone that needs a quick bite for 7 or 8 bucks, i rather take the business to Wendy's down the street.

To the franchise owner:
Please fix these problem.  Customers have choice.  I choose not to ever go back there AGAIN<//Review>
